`github/static/js/record.js`:\n\n```javascript\nlet recordingState = {\n    currentStep: 'title',\n    titleSegments: [],\n    bodySegments: [],\n    isRecording: false,\n    startTime: null,\n    timerInterval: null\n};\n\n// Запись заголовка\ndocument.getElementById('btn-record-title').addEventListener('click', async function() {\n    if (!recordingState.isRecording) {\n        // Начать запись\n        recordingState.isRecording = true;\n        recordingState.startTime = Date.now();\n        this.textContent = '⏹️ Остановить запись';\n        this.classList.add('recording');\n\n        // Показать таймер\n        document.getElementById('timer-title').style.display = 'block';\n        startTimer('timer-title');\n\n        // Начать получение данных от OMI\n        await startRecordingSession(sessionId, 'title');\n    } else {\n        // Остановить запись\n        recordingState.isRecording = false;\n        this.textContent = '🎤 Записать заголовок';\n        this.classList.remove('recording');\n\n        stopTimer();\n\n        // Остановить сессию и получить текст\n        const text = await stopRecordingSession(sessionId, 'title');\n\n        // Показать предпросмотр\n        document.getElementById('text-title').value = text;\n        document.getElementById('preview-title').style.display = 'block';\n    }\n});\n\n// Подтверждение заголовка\nfunction confirmTitle() {\n    const title = document.getElementById('text-title').value;\n\n    if (!title.trim()) {\n        alert('Пожалуйста, введите заголовок');\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Сохраним заголовок\n    recordingState.title = title;\n\n    // Покажем его в следующем разделе\n    document.getElementById('confirmed-title-text').textContent = title;\n\n    // Переключаем на запись body\n    document.getElementById('section-title').style.display = 'none';\n    document.getElementById('section-body').style.display = 'block';\n\n    // Обновляем индикатор прогресса\n    document.getElementById('step-1').removeAttribute('data-active');\n    document.getElementById('step-2').setAttribute('data-active', 'true');\n}\n\n// Запись описания (аналогично title)\ndocument.getElementById('btn-record-body').addEventListener('click', async function() {\n    // Аналогично btn-record-title...\n});\n\n// Подтверждение описания\nfunction confirmBody() {\n    const body = document.getElementById('text-body').value;\n\n    if (!body.trim()) {\n        alert('Пожалуйста, введите описание');\n        return;\n    }\n\n    recordingState.body = body;\n\n    // Показываем финальный предпросмотр\n    document.getElementById('final-title').textContent = recordingState.title;\n    document.getElementById('final-body').textContent = recordingState.body;\n\n    document.getElementById('section-body').style.display = 'none';\n    document.getElementById('section-final').style.display = 'block';\n\n    document.getElementById('step-2').removeAttribute('data-active');\n    document.getElementById('step-3').setAttribute('data-active', 'true');\n}\n\n// Создание Issue\nasync function createIssue() {\n    const btn = event.target;\n    btn.disabled = true;\n    btn.textContent = 'Создаем...';\n\n    try {\n        const response = await fetch('/api/create-issue', {\n            method: 'POST',\n            headers: {\n                'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n            },\n            body: JSON.stringify({\n                repo: repo,\n                title: recordingState.title,\n                body: recordingState.body,\n                session_id: sessionId\n            })\n        });\n\n        const result = await response.json();\n\n        if (result.success) {\n            // Перенаправляем на страницу успеха\n            window.location.href = `/success?issue_url=${encodeURIComponent(result.issue_url)}&lang=${lang}`;\n        } else {\n            alert(`Ошибка: ${result.error}`);\n            btn.disabled = false;\n            btn.textContent = '🚀 Создать Issue';\n        }\n    } catch (error) {\n        alert(`Ошибка: ${error.message}`);\n        btn.disabled = false;\n        btn.textContent = '🚀 Создать Issue';\n    }\n}\n\n// Вспомогательные функции\nfunction startTimer(elementId) {\n    recordingState.timerInterval = setInterval(() => {\n        const elapsed = Math.floor((Date.now() - recordingState.startTime) / 1000);\n        const minutes = Math.floor(elapsed / 60);\n        const seconds = elapsed % 60;\n        document.getElementById(elementId).textContent =\n            `${minutes}:${seconds.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;\n    }, 1000);\n}\n\nfunction stopTimer() {\n    if (recordingState.timerInterval) {\n        clearInterval(recordingState.timerInterval);\n        recordingState.timerInterval = null;\n    }\n}\n\nasync function startRecordingSession(sessionId, type) {\n    // Отправляем на сервер, что началась запись\n    await fetch(`/api/sessions/${sessionId}/${type}/start`, {\n        method: 'POST'\n    });\n}\n\nasync function stopRecordingSession(sessionId, type) {\n    // Останавливаем запись и получаем текст\n    const response = await fetch(`/api/sessions/${sessionId}/${type}/stop`, {\n        method: 'POST'\n    });\n    const result = await response.json();\n    return result.text;\n}\n\nfunction recordTitleAgain() {\n    document.getElementById('preview-title').style.display = 'none';\n    document.getElementById('text-title').value = '';\n    recordingState.titleSegments = [];\n}\n\nfunction recordBodyAgain() {\n    document.getElementById('preview-body').style.display = 'none';\n    document.getElementById('text-body').value = '';\n    recordingState.bodySegments = [];\n}\n\nfunction editTitle() {\n    document.getElementById('section-final').style.display = 'none';\n    document.getElementById('section-title').style.display = 'block';\n    document.getElementById('preview-title').style.display = 'block';\n    document.getElementById('step-3').removeAttribute('data-active');\n    document.getElementById('step-1').setAttribute('data-active', 'true');\n}\n\nfunction editBody() {\n    document.getElementById('section-final').style.display = 'none';\n    document.getElementById('section-body').style.display = 'block';\n    document.getElementById('preview-body').style.display = 'block';\n    document.getElementById('step-3').removeAttribute('data-active');\n    document.getElementById('step-2').setAttribute('data-active', 'true');\n}\n\nasync function saveDraft() {\n    const response = await fetch('/api/drafts', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {\n            'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n        },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n            repo: repo,\n            title: recordingState.title,\n            body: recordingState.body\n        })\n    });\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n\n    if (result.success) {\n        alert('Черновик сохранен');\n        window.location.href = `/?lang=${lang}`;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Этап 5: Обновление backend логики\n\n### 5.1 Управление сессиями\n\nСоздайте `github/session_manager.py`:\n\n```python\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom enum import Enum\nimport time\n\nclass SessionState(Enum):\n    IDLE = \"idle\"\n    RECORDING_TITLE = \"recording_title\"\n    PREVIEW_TITLE = \"preview_title\"\n    RECORDING_BODY = \"recording_body\"\n    PREVIEW_BODY = \"preview_body\"\n    FINAL_PREVIEW = \"final_preview\"\n    CREATING_ISSUE = \"creating_issue\"\n    COMPLETED = \"completed\"\n\n@dataclass\nclass RecordingSession:\n    session_id: str\n    user_id: str\n    repo: str\n    state: SessionState = SessionState.IDLE\n    title_segments: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    body_segments: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    title_text: str = \"\"\n    body_text: str = \"\"\n    created_at: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    last_activity: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n\n    def start_title_recording(self):\n        self.state = SessionState.RECORDING_TITLE\n        self.title_segments = []\n        self.last_activity = time.time()\n\n    def stop_title_recording(self):\n        self.state = SessionState.PREVIEW_TITLE\n        # Объедините сегменты в текст\n        self.title_text = \" \".join(seg[\"text\"] for seg in self.title_segments)\n        self.last_activity = time.time()\n\n    def confirm_title(self, title: str):\n        self.title_text = title\n        self.state = SessionState.IDLE\n        self.last_activity = time.time()\n\n    def start_body_recording(self):\n        self.state = SessionState.RECORDING_BODY\n        self.body_segments = []\n        self.last_activity = time.time()\n\n    def stop_body_recording(self):\n        self.state = SessionState.PREVIEW_BODY\n        self.body_text = \" \".join(seg[\"text\"] for seg in self.body_segments)\n        self.last_activity = time.time()\n\n    def confirm_body(self, body: str):\n        self.body_text = body\n        self.state = SessionState.FINAL_PREVIEW\n        self.last_activity = time.time()\n\n    def is_expired(self, timeout: int = 1800) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Проверка, истек ли timeout сессии (по умолчанию 30 минут)\"\"\"\n        return time.time() - self.last_activity > timeout\n\nclass SessionManager:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.sessions: Dict[str, RecordingSession] = {}\n\n    def create_session(self, session_id: str, user_id: str, repo: str) -> RecordingSession:\n        session = RecordingSession(\n            session_id=session_id,\n            user_id=user_id,\n            repo=repo\n        )\n        self.sessions[session_id] = session\n        return session\n\n    def get_session(self, session_id: str) -> Optional[RecordingSession]:\n        return self.sessions.get(session_id)\n\n    def delete_session(self, session_id: str):\n        if session_id in self.sessions:\n            del self.sessions[session_id]\n\n    def cleanup_expired_sessions(self):\n        \"\"\"Удаление истекших сессий\"\"\"\n        expired = [\n            sid for sid, session in self.sessions.items()\n            if session.is_expired()\n        ]\n        for sid in expired:\n            del self.sessions[sid]\n\n# Глобальный менеджер сессий\nsession_manager = SessionManager()\n```\n\n### 5.2 Обновление webhook handler\n\nОбновите `main.py` для обработки вебхуков с учетом сессий:\n\n```python\nfrom fastapi import FastAPI, Request\nfrom github.session_manager import session_manager, SessionState\n\n@app.post(\"/webhook\")\nasync def handle_webhook(request: Request):\n    \"\"\"\n    Обработка вебхуков от OMI\n    \"\"\"\n    session_id = request.query_params.get(\"session_id\")\n    uid = request.query_params.get(\"uid\")\n\n    # Получите сессию\n    session = session_manager.get_session(session_id)\n\n    if not session:\n        return {\"status\": \"error\", \"message\": \"Session not found\"}\n\n    # Получите данные\n    data = await request.json()\n    segments = data.get(\"segments\", [])\n\n    # Обработайте в зависимости от состояния\n    if session.state == SessionState.RECORDING_TITLE:\n        # Добавьте сегменты к title\n        session.title_segments.extend(segments)\n        session.last_activity = time.time()\n        return {\"status\": \"recording\", \"segment_count\": len(session.title_segments)}\n\n    elif session.state == SessionState.RECORDING_BODY:\n        # Добавьте сегменты к body\n        session.body_segments.extend(segments)\n        session.last_activity = time.time()\n        return {\"status\": \"recording\", \"segment_count\": len(session.body_segments)}\n\n    else:\n        return {\"status\": \"ignored\", \"reason\": \"not_recording\"}\n```\n\n### 5.3 API эндпоинты для управления сессией\n\n```python\n@app.post(\"/api/sessions/{session_id}/title/start\")\nasync def start_title_recording(session_id: str):\n    session = session_manager.get_session(session_id)\n    if not session:\n        return {\"success\": False, \"error\": \"Session not found\"}\n\n    session.start_title_recording()\n    return {\"success\": True, \"state\": session.state.value}\n\n@app.post(\"/api/sessions/{session_id}/title/stop\")\nasync def stop_title_recording(session_id: str):\n    session = session_manager.get_session(session_id)\n    if not session:\n        return {\"success\": False, \"error\": \"Session not found\"}\n\n    session.stop_title_recording()\n    return {\"success\": True, \"text\": session.title_text}\n\n@app.post(\"/api/sessions/{session_id}/body/start\")\nasync def start_body_recording(session_id: str):\n    session = session_manager.get_session(session_id)\n    if not session:\n        return {\"success\": False, \"error\": \"Session not found\"}\n\n    session.start_body_recording()\n    return {\"success\": True, \"state\": session.state.value}\n\n@app.post(\"/api/sessions/{session_id}/body/stop\")\nasync def stop_body_recording(session_id: str):\n    session = session_manager.get_session(session_id)\n    if not session:\n        return {\"success\": False, \"error\": \"Session not found\"}\n\n    session.stop_body_recording()\n    return {\"success\": True, \"text\": session.body_text}\n\n@app.post(\"/api/create-issue\")\nasync def create_issue_endpoint(request: Request):\n    data = await request.json()\n\n    repo = data[\"repo\"]\n    title = data[\"title\"]\n    body = data[\"body\"]\n    session_id = data[\"session_id\"]\n\n    # Получите GitHub token пользователя\n    session = session_manager.get_session(session_id)\n    uid = session.user_id\n    github_token = get_user_github_token(uid)\n\n    # Создайте Issue\n    from github import Github\n    g = Github(github_token)\n    repository = g.get_repo(repo)\n\n    issue = repository.create_issue(\n        title=title,\n        body=body,\n        labels=[\"from-omi-improved\"]\n    )\n\n    # Очистите сессию\n    session_manager.delete_session(session_id)\n\n    return {\n        \"success\": True,\n        \"issue_url\": issue.html_url,\n        \"issue_number\": issue.number\n    }\n```\n\n## Этап 6: Тестирование\n\n### 6.1 Локальное тестирование\n\n```bash\n# Выберите репозиторий\n5. Нажмите \"Создать Issue голосом\"\n6. Запишите заголовок (через OMI или введите вручную)\n7. Подтвердите заголовок\n8. Запишите описание\n9. Подтвердите описание\n10. Отредактируйте в текстовом поле\n3. Подтвердите\n4. Продолжайте процесс\n\n**Тест 3: Переключение языков**\n1. Откройте главную страницу\n2. Переключите язык на English\n3.
